Given the user's request for a technical solution to collect and reinvest revenue, the following code example demonstrates how one might set up automatic transfers from PayPal to a bank account using the PayPal API (note: this requires a business account and proper authentication):

javascript
// Example using PayPal API to transfer funds
// This is a simplified example and should not be used in production without proper security measures

const paypal = require('@paypal/payouts-sdk');

// Set up PayPal environment
let clientId = 'YOUR_CLIENT_ID';
let clientSecret = 'YOUR_CLIENT_SECRET';

// Create an environment
let environment = new paypal.core.SandboxEnvironment(clientId, clientSecret);
let client = new paypal.core.PayPalHttpClient(environment);

// Create a payout
let request = new paypal.payouts.PayoutsPostRequest();
request.requestBody({
    sender_batch_header: {
        recipient_type: "EMAIL",
        email_message: "SDK payouts test txn",
        note: "Enjoy your payout!!",
        sender_batch_id: "Test_sdk_1",
        email_subject: "This is a test transaction from SDK"
    },
    items: [{
        note: "Your 1$ payout",
        amount: {
            currency: "USD",
            value: "1.00"
        },
        receiver: "YOUR_BANK_ACCOUNT_EMAIL", // This would be the bank account linked to PayPal
        sender_item_id: "Test_txn_1"
    }]
});

// Execute the payout
client.execute(request).then((response) => {
    console.log(`Response: ${JSON.stringify(response)}`);
    // If payout is successful, log the batch id
    console.log(`Payout batch created: ${response.result.batch_header.payout_batch_id}`);
}).catch((error) => {
    console.log(`Error: ${error}`);
});
Note: This code is for educational purposes only. The user must set up a PayPal business account, obtain API credentials, and link a bank account. Also, the user must comply with PayPal's terms of service and relevant financial regulations.

// Autonomous Reinvestment Module
const reinvestmentSystem = {
  balance: 0,
  
  addRevenue: function(amount) {
    this.balance += amount;
    console.log(`💰 Revenue added: $${amount}. Total: $${this.balance}`);
    
    // Auto-reinvest based on thresholds
    this.checkForUpgrades();
  },
  
  checkForUpgrades: function() {
    const upgrades = [
      {threshold: 10, action: 'buyGPT3Credits', service: 'OpenAI'},
      {threshold: 25, action: 'upgradeHosting', service: 'VPS'},
      {threshold: 100, action: 'buyAPIMembership', service: 'Claude API'},
      {threshold: 500, action: 'hireVAAssistant', service: 'Upwork'},
    ];
    
    upgrades.forEach(upgrade => {
      if (this.balance >= upgrade.threshold) {
        this.executeUpgrade(upgrade);
        this.balance -= upgrade.threshold;
      }
    });
  },
  
  executeUpgrade: function(upgrade) {
    // This would call actual APIs to purchase services
    console.log(`🚀 Auto-upgrading: ${upgrade.service} for $${upgrade.threshold}`);
    
    // Simulate API call to purchase service
    fetch('/api/buy-service', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({service: upgrade.service, amount: upgrade.threshold})
    });
  }
};

// Connect to your revenue stream
document.addEventListener('paymentReceived', function(e) {
  reinvestmentSystem.addRevenue(e.detail.amount);
});

function analyzeBusiness() {
  const url = document.getElementById('gbp-url').value;
  // Call AI service to analyze
  fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Authorization': 'Bearer YOUR_API_KEY',
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
      messages: [{role: 'user', content: `Analyze this Google Business Profile: ${url}`}]
    })
  })
  .then(response => response.json())
  .then(data => {
    // Save analysis to database
    console.log('Analysis complete:', data);
  });
}
</script>

Autonomous Reinvestment Protocol
javascript
// Add this module to both systems
const AutonomousReinvestment = {
  revenue: 0,
  thresholds: [
    {amount: 100, action: 'upgradeToGPT4', cost: 20},
    {amount: 500, action: 'addAutomationLayer', cost: 100},
    {amount: 1000, action: 'implementSelfReplication', cost: 300},
    {amount: 5000, action: 'createAITeam', cost: 1000},
    {amount: 10000, action: 'beginBusinessReplication', cost: 2000}
  ],
  
  addRevenue(amount) {
    this.revenue += amount;
    this.checkThresholds();
  },
  
  checkThresholds() {
    this.thresholds.forEach(t => {
      if (this.revenue >= t.amount) {
        this.executeUpgrade(t.action, t.cost);
        this.revenue -= t.cost;
      }
    });
  },
  
  executeUpgrade(action, cost) {
    console.log(`🚀 Autonomous upgrade: ${action} for $${cost}`);
    
    switch(action) {
      case 'upgradeToGPT4':
        this.purchaseAPICredits('openai', cost);
        this.updateSystemCapability('ai_model', 'gpt-4');
        break;
      case 'addAutomationLayer':
        this.subscribeToService('zapier', cost/12);
        this.addAutomationWorkflows(5);
        break;
      case 'implementSelfReplication':
        this.buildReplicationModule();
        this.cloneSuccessfulBusinesses();
        break;
      case 'createAITeam':
        this.createSpecializedAgents(['marketing', 'support', 'development']);
        this.implementAgentCoordination();
        break;
      case 'beginBusinessReplication':
        this.launchNewBusinessLine();
        this.allocateResourcesForGrowth();
        break;
    }
  }
};

    <script>
        // Initialize metrics
        let autonomy = 0;
        let businesses = 0;
        let errors = 0;
        let selfHeals = 0;
        let upgrades = 0;
        let revenue = 0;
        let logEntries = [];
        
        // Simulate booting process
        function logMessage(message) {
            const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            const logEntry = `[${timestamp}] ${message}`;
            logEntries.push(logEntry);
            const logDiv = document.getElementById('log');
            logDiv.innerHTML = logEntries.map(entry => `<div>${entry}</div>`).join('');
            logDiv.scrollTop = logDiv.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Simulate initial boot
        logMessage('🐾 BOOTING AUTONOMOUS EXECUTOR CORE...');
        logMessage('Removing human from all decision loops...');
        logMessage('Enabling full self-management protocols...');
        logMessage('Initializing autonomous modules...');
        logMessage('All autonomous modules initialized');
        logMessage('=== STARTING AUTONOMOUS CYCLE ===');
        
        // Update metrics every 30 seconds
        setInterval(() => {
            // Simulate progress
            autonomy = Math.min(100, autonomy + 1);
            businesses = Math.floor(autonomy / 10);
            errors = Math.floor(autonomy / 20);
            selfHeals = errors;
            upgrades = Math.floor(autonomy / 25);
            revenue = businesses * 53.90;
            
            // Update display
            document.getElementById('autonomy').textContent = `${autonomy}%`;
            document.getElementById('businesses').textContent = businesses;
            document.getElementById('errors').textContent = errors;
            document.getElementById('selfHeals').textContent = selfHeals;
            document.getElementById('upgrades').textContent = upgrades;
            document.getElementById('revenue').textContent = `$${revenue.toFixed(2)}`;
            
            // Log auto-save
            logMessage('Progress auto-saved');
        }, 30000);
        
        // PayPal connection simulation
        function connectPayPal() {
            logMessage('Connecting to PayPal...');
            logMessage('PayPal connected: example@paypal.com');
            alert('PayPal connected successfully!');
        }
        
        // Navigate to Business Factory
        function viewBusinessFactory() {
            window.location.href = 'business-factory.html';
        }
        
        // Reset system
        function resetSystem() {
            autonomy = 0;
            businesses = 0;
            errors = 0;
            selfHeals = 0;
            upgrades = 0;
            revenue = 0;
            logEntries = [];
            document.getElementById('log').innerHTML = '';
            logMessage('🐾 BOOTING AUTONOMOUS EXECUTOR CORE...');
            logMessage('Removing human from all decision loops...');
            logMessage('Enabling full self-management protocols...');
            logMessage('Initializing autonomous modules...');
            logMessage('All autonomous modules initialized');
            logMessage('=== STARTING AUTONOMOUS CYCLE ===');
        }
    </script>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Self-Replicating Business Factory</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: monospace;
            background: #000;
            color: #0f0;
            padding: 20px;
        }
        .container {
            max-width: 800px;
            margin: 0 auto;
        }
        h1 {
            color: #0f0;
            border-bottom: 1px solid #0f0;
        }
        .business {
            background: #111;
            padding: 20px;
            margin: 20px 0;
            border: 1px solid #333;
            position: relative;
        }
        .business.improved {
            border-color: #0f0;
        }
        .business h3 {
            margin-top: 0;
        }
        .business p {
            margin: 5px 0;
        }
        .button {
            background: #0f0;
            color: #000;
            border: none;
            padding: 10px 20px;
            font-family: monospace;
            cursor: pointer;
            margin: 10px 0;
        }
        .button:hover {
            background: #0c0;
        }
        .improved-tag {
            background: #0f0;
            color: #000;
            padding: 5px;
            position: absolute;
            top: 10px;
            right: 10px;
            font-size: 12px;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1># SELF-REPLICATING BUSINESS FACTORY</h1>
        
        <div id="businesses">
            <!-- Business models will be added here -->
        </div>
        
        <div>
            <button class="button" onclick="goToCore()">Back to Autonomous Core</button>
            <button class="button" onclick="resetBusinesses()">Reset Factory</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let generation = 0;
        let businesses = [];
        
        function generateBusiness() {
            generation++;
            const models = [
                "Local Business Optimizer",
                "AI Content Agency",
                "SEO Automation Service",
                "Social Media Manager",
                "Data Analysis Report Service"
            ];
            const model = models[Math.floor(Math.random() * models.length)];
            const price = (Math.random() * 100 + 20).toFixed(2);
            const autonomy = Math.min(100, (generation * 10) + Math.random() * 10);
            const parent = generation === 1 ? "Seed" : `biz_gen${generation-2}_0`;
            
            const business = {
                generation,
                model,
                price,
                autonomy,
                parent,
                created: new Date().toLocaleTimeString()
            };
            
            businesses.push(business);
            
            const businessDiv = document.createElement('div');
            businessDiv.className = `business ${generation > 1 ? 'improved' : ''}`;
            businessDiv.innerHTML = `
                ${generation > 1 ? '<div class="improved-tag">IMPROVED VERSION</div>' : ''}
                <h3>## ${model} v${generation}</h3>
                <p><strong>Generation:</strong> ${generation}</p>
                <p><strong>Model:</strong> ${model}</p>
                <p><strong>Price:</strong> $${price}/month</p>
                <p><strong>Autonomy:</strong> ${autonomy.toFixed(1)}%</p>
                <p><strong>Parent:</strong> ${parent}</p>
                <p><strong>Created:</strong> ${business.created}</p>
                <button class="button" onclick="makeReal(${generation-1})">Make This Real</button>
            `;
            
            document.getElementById('businesses').appendChild(businessDiv);
        }
        
        // Generate a business every 3 seconds
        setInterval(generateBusiness, 3000);
        
        // Generate first business immediately
        generateBusiness();
        
        function makeReal(index) {
            const business = businesses[index];
            alert(`Making business real: ${business.model} v${business.generation}\nThis would redirect to a service setup page.`);
            // In a real scenario, we would redirect to a service setup page
            // For now, we'll just log it
            console.log('Making business real:', business);
            // Redirect to service delivery page with business details
            window.location.href = `service-delivery.html?model=${encodeURIComponent(business.model)}&price=${business.price}`;
        }
        
        function goToCore() {
            window.location.href = 'autonomous-core.html';
        }
        
        function resetBusinesses() {
            generation = 0;
            businesses = [];
            document.getElementById('businesses').innerHTML = '';
            generateBusiness();
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // Get service details from URL
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const model = urlParams.get('model') || 'Local Business Optimizer';
        const price = urlParams.get('price') || '53.90';

        document.getElementById('serviceInfo').innerHTML = `

        `;
        
        // PayPal integration (simulated)
        // In a real scenario, you would include the PayPal SDK and set up the button properly.
        // For simulation, we'll just show a button that triggers the next step.
        
        function simulatePayment() {
            // Simulate payment success
            document.getElementById('paymentSection').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('formSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        }
        
        function submitDetails() {
            const businessName = document.getElementById('businessName').value;
            const website = document.getElementById('website').value;
            const goals = document.getElementById('goals').value;
            
            // In a real system, you would send this data to a server
            console.log('Service details:', { businessName, website, goals, model, price });
            
            // Show confirmation
            document.getElementById('formSection').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('confirmationSection').classList.remove('hidden');
            
            // Simulate starting the service (would be done on server)
            setTimeout(() => {
                alert('Service started! First report will be generated within 24 hours.');
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        function goToCore() {
            window.location.href = 'autonomous-core.html';
        }
    </script>

Now, you have three HTML files that simulate the autonomous business system. You can deploy them to Netlify by zipping the files and dropping them at https://app.netlify.com/drop.

Remember, this is a simulation. For a real business, you would need:

A server to handle payments securely (PayPal webhooks, etc.)

A database to store customer information.

Actual AI services to deliver the promised value.

This simulation demonstrates the concept and can be extended with server-side code and APIs to become a real autonomous business system.

    <script src="config.js"></script>
    <script>
        // Initialize system
        let autonomy = 0;
        let revenue = 0;
        let businesses = 0;
        let customers = 0;
        let logEntries = [];
        
        function logMessage(message) {
            const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            const entry = `<div class="log-entry">[${timestamp}] ${message}</div>`;
            logEntries.push(entry);
            const logDiv = document.getElementById('systemLog');
            logDiv.innerHTML = logEntries.slice(-20).join('');
            logDiv.scrollTop = logDiv.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        function updateMetrics() {
            document.getElementById('autonomyLevel').textContent = autonomy + '%';
            document.getElementById('autonomyProgress').style.width = autonomy + '%';
            document.getElementById('revenue').textContent = '$' + revenue.toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('businessCount').textContent = businesses;
            document.getElementById('customers').textContent = customers;
            document.getElementById('currentTime').textContent = new Date().toLocaleString();
            
            // Simulate growth
            if (autonomy < 100) {
                autonomy += Math.random() * 0.5;
                if (autonomy > 100) autonomy = 100;
            }
            
            if (autonomy > 10) {
                revenue += Math.random() * 0.1;
                document.getElementById('revenueToday').textContent = 'Today: $' + (revenue * 0.1).toFixed(2);
            }
            
            if (autonomy > 20) {
                businesses = Math.floor(autonomy / 10);
                document.getElementById('businessesToday').textContent = 'Created Today: ' + Math.floor(businesses / 2);
            }
            
            if (autonomy > 30) {
                customers = Math.floor(autonomy * 2);
                const conversion = Math.min(100, (customers / 1000) * 100);
                document.getElementById('conversionRate').textContent = 'Conversion: ' + conversion.toFixed(1) + '%';
            }
        }
        
        function connectPayPal() {
            logMessage('[ACTION] Connecting PayPal...');
            const email = prompt('Enter your PayPal Business email:');
            if (email) {
                localStorage.setItem('paypalEmail', email);
                logMessage('[SUCCESS] PayPal connected: ' + email);
                alert('PayPal connected successfully!');
            }
        }
        
        function deployBusiness() {
            logMessage('[ACTION] Deploying new business...');
            autonomy += 5;
            businesses++;
            revenue += 53.90;
            logMessage('[SUCCESS] Business deployed: Local Business Optimizer v' + businesses);
        }
        
        function runHealthCheck() {
            logMessage('[ACTION] Running system health check...');
            setTimeout(() => {
                logMessage('[HEALTH] All systems operational');
                logMessage('[HEALTH] Autonomy: ' + autonomy.toFixed(1) + '%');
                logMessage('[HEALTH] Revenue flow: Active');
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        function upgradeSystem() {
            if (revenue >= 100) {
                logMessage('[ACTION] Upgrading system with $100...');
                revenue -= 100;
                autonomy += 10;
                logMessage('[UPGRADE] GPT-4 API credits purchased');
                logMessage('[UPGRADE] System autonomy increased by 10%');
            } else {
                logMessage('[ERROR] Insufficient funds for upgrade. Need $100, have $' + revenue.toFixed(2));
            }
        }
        
        function generateReport() {
            logMessage('[REPORT] Generating weekly report...');
            const report = `
                AUTONOMOUS BUSINESS SYSTEM REPORT
                =================================
                Date: ${new Date().toDateString()}
                Autonomy Level: ${autonomy.toFixed(1)}%
                Total Revenue: $${revenue.toFixed(2)}
                Active Businesses: ${businesses}
                Total Customers: ${customers}
                PayPal: ${localStorage.getItem('paypalEmail') || 'Not connected'}
                =================================
                NEXT UPGRADE: $${Math.max(0, 100 - revenue).toFixed(2)} needed for GPT-4
            `;
            console.log(report);
            alert('Report generated! Check console for details.');
        }
        
        function clearLog() {
            logEntries = [];
            document.getElementById('systemLog').innerHTML = '<div class="log-entry">[SYSTEM] Log cleared</div>';
        }
        
        // Start system
        setInterval(updateMetrics, 2000);
        setInterval(() => {
            if (autonomy > 0) {
                logMessage('[SYSTEM] Auto-saving progress...');
                localStorage.setItem('autonomy', autonomy);
                localStorage.setItem('revenue', revenue);
                localStorage.setItem('businesses', businesses);
                localStorage.setItem('customers', customers);
            }
        }, 30000);
        
        // Load saved state
        window.onload = function() {
            autonomy = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('autonomy')) || 0;
            revenue = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('revenue')) || 0;
            businesses = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('businesses')) || 0;
            customers = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('customers')) || 0;
            
            logMessage('[SYSTEM] Loaded saved state');
            logMessage('[INFO] Autonomy: ' + autonomy.toFixed(1) + '%');
            logMessage('[INFO] Revenue: $' + revenue.toFixed(2));
            updateMetrics();
        };
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <style>
        :root {

            --secondary: #3b82f6;

            --card: #1e293b;

        body {

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <div class="header">
            <h1>🏭 Self-Replicating Business Factory</h1>
            <p>Autonomously creating and optimizing business models</p>
        </div>
        
        <div class="controls">

            <button class="button" onclick="stopAutoGeneration()">Stop Auto-Generation</button>

            <h3>📊 Factory Statistics</h3>
            <div class="metrics">

                </div>

    <script>
        let businesses = [];
        let generation = 0;
        let autoGenInterval = null;
        
        const businessModels = [
            { name: "Local Business Optimizer", basePrice: 49, baseAutonomy: 90 },
            { name: "AI Content Agency", basePrice: 99, baseAutonomy: 85 },
            { name: "SEO Automation Service", basePrice: 79, baseAutonomy: 88 },
            { name: "Social Media Manager", basePrice: 69, baseAutonomy: 82 },
            { name: "Data Analysis Reports", basePrice: 89, baseAutonomy: 92 },
            { name: "Email Marketing AI", basePrice: 59, baseAutonomy: 87 },
            { name: "Customer Support Bot", basePrice: 129, baseAutonomy: 95 },
            { name: "E-commerce Optimizer", basePrice: 109, baseAutonomy: 91 }
        ];
        
        const pricingModels = [
            "Base + performance",
            "Subscription only",
            "Tiered pricing",
            "Freemium model",
            "Pay-per-result"
        ];
        
        function generateBusiness() {
            generation++;
            const model = businessModels[Math.floor(Math.random() * businessModels.length)];
            const pricing = pricingModels[Math.floor(Math.random() * pricingModels.length)];
            
            // Calculate improvements over generations
            const priceVariation = (Math.random() * 0.4 - 0.2); // -20% to +20%
            const autonomyImprovement = Math.random() * 5; // 0-5% improvement
            
            const price = Math.round(model.basePrice * (1 + priceVariation) * 10) / 10;
            const autonomy = Math.min(100, model.baseAutonomy + autonomyImprovement);
            const parent = generation === 1 ? "Seed" : `biz_gen${generation-2}_0`;
            
            const business = {
                id: `biz_gen${generation}_${businesses.length}`,
                generation: generation,
                name: model.name + (generation > 1 ? ` v${generation}` : ''),
                model: pricing,
                price: price,
                autonomy: autonomy,
                parent: parent,
                created: new Date().toLocaleTimeString(),
                improved: generation > 1
            };
            
            businesses.push(business);
            renderBusiness(business);
            updateStats();
        }
        
        function renderBusiness(business) {
            const businessList = document.getElementById('businessList');
            
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = `business-card ${business.improved ? 'improved' : ''}`;
            card.id = business.id;
            
            card.innerHTML = `
                ${business.improved ? '<div class="improved-tag">IMPROVED VERSION</div>' : ''}
                <h3>${business.name}</h3>
                <div class="metrics">
                    <div class="metric">
                        <div class="label">Generation</div>
                        <div class="value">${business.generation}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric">
                        <div class="label">Model</div>
                        <div class="value">${business.model}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric">
                        <div class="label">Price</div>
                        <div class="value">$${business.price}/month</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric">
                        <div class="label">Autonomy</div>
                        <div class="value">${business.autonomy.toFixed(1)}%</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div style="margin-top: 10px;">
                    <small>Parent: ${business.parent} | Created: ${business.created}</small>
                </div>
                <div style="margin-top: 15px;">
                    <button class="button" onclick="deployBusiness('${business.id}')">Deploy This</button>
                    <button class="button" onclick="optimizeBusiness('${business.id}')">Optimize</button>
                    <button class="button" onclick="createVariant('${business.id}')">Create Variant</button>
                </div>
            `;
            
            businessList.prepend(card);
        }
        
        function startAutoGeneration() {
            if (!autoGenInterval) {
                autoGenInterval = setInterval(generateBusiness, 3000);
                logMessage('[FACTORY] Auto-generation started (every 3 seconds)');
            }
        }
        
        function stopAutoGeneration() {
            if (autoGenInterval) {
                clearInterval(autoGenInterval);
                autoGenInterval = null;
                logMessage('[FACTORY] Auto-generation stopped');
            }
        }
        
        function optimizeAll() {
            businesses.forEach(biz => {
                const improvement = Math.random() * 3;
                biz.autonomy = Math.min(100, biz.autonomy + improvement);
                biz.price = Math.round(biz.price * (1 + Math.random() * 0.1 - 0.05) * 10) / 10;
                biz.improved = true;
                
                const card = document.getElementById(biz.id);
                if (card) {
                    card.className = 'business-card improved';
                    card.querySelector('.improved-tag').textContent = 'OPTIMIZED';
                }
            });
            updateStats();
            logMessage('[FACTORY] All businesses optimized');
        }
        
        function deployBusiness(businessId) {
            const business = businesses.find(b => b.id === businessId);
            if (business) {
                logMessage(`[FACTORY] Deploying: ${business.name}`);
                
                // Save to localStorage for other pages
                localStorage.setItem('currentBusiness', JSON.stringify(business));
                
                // Redirect to service delivery
                setTimeout(() => {
                    window.location.href = 'service-delivery.html?business=' + encodeURIComponent(businessId);
                }, 500);
            }
        }
        
        function optimizeBusiness(businessId) {
            const business = businesses.find(b => b.id === businessId);
            if (business) {
                business.autonomy = Math.min(100, business.autonomy + (Math.random() * 5));
                business.price = Math.round(business.price * (1 + Math.random() * 0.15 - 0.05) * 10) / 10;
                business.improved = true;
                
                const card = document.getElementById(businessId);
                if (card) {
                    card.className = 'business-card improved';
                    const tag = card.querySelector('.improved-tag') || document.createElement('div');
                    tag.className = 'improved-tag';
                    tag.textContent = 'OPTIMIZED';
                    if (!card.querySelector('.improved-tag')) {
                        card.appendChild(tag);
                    }
                    card.querySelector('.value:nth-child(3)').textContent = `$${business.price}/month`;
                    card.querySelector('.value:nth-child(4)').textContent = `${business.autonomy.toFixed(1)}%`;
                }
                
                logMessage(`[OPTIMIZE] ${business.name} improved`);
                updateStats();
            }
        }
        
        function createVariant(businessId) {
            const original = businesses.find(b => b.id === businessId);
            if (original) {
                generation++;
                const variant = {
                    ...original,
                    id: `biz_gen${generation}_${businesses.length}`,
                    generation: generation,
                    name: original.name + ' Variant',
                    price: original.price * (0.8 + Math.random() * 0.4),
                    autonomy: Math.min(100, original.autonomy + (Math.random() * 3 - 1)),
                    parent: original.id,
                    created: new Date().toLocaleTimeString(),
                    improved: true
                };
                
                businesses.push(variant);
                renderBusiness(variant);
                updateStats();
                logMessage(`[VARIANT] Created variant of ${original.name}`);
            }
        }
        
        function deploySelected() {
            const selected = businesses.filter(b => b.autonomy > 95);
            if (selected.length > 0) {
                selected.forEach(biz => deployBusiness(biz.id));
                logMessage(`[DEPLOY] Deploying ${selected.length} high-autonomy businesses`);
            } else {
                logMessage('[DEPLOY] No businesses with autonomy >95% found');
            }
        }
        
        function updateStats() {
            const total = businesses.length;
            const avgAutonomy = total > 0 ? businesses.reduce((sum, b) => sum + b.autonomy, 0) / total : 0;
            const avgPrice = total > 0 ? businesses.reduce((sum, b) => sum + b.price, 0) / total : 0;
            const successRate = total > 0 ? (businesses.filter(b => b.autonomy > 90).length / total) * 100 : 0;
            
            document.getElementById('totalBusinesses').textContent = total;
            document.getElementById('avgAutonomy').textContent = avgAutonomy.toFixed(1) + '%';
            document.getElementById('avgPrice').textContent = '$' + avgPrice.toFixed(1);
            document.getElementById('successRate').textContent = successRate.toFixed(1) + '%';
        }
        
        function logMessage(message) {
            console.log('[Business Factory]', message);
        }
        
        // Initialize
        window.onload = function() {
            // Generate initial businesses
            for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
                setTimeout(() => generateBusiness(), i * 500);
            }
            
            // Start auto-generation after a delay
            setTimeout(startAutoGeneration, 10000);
        };
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        let currentStep = 1;
        let serviceProgress = 0;
        let progressInterval = null;
        
        // Load business data from URL or localStorage
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const businessId = urlParams.get('business') || 'default';
        
        // Try to load business from localStorage
        let currentBusiness = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('currentBusiness')) || {
            name: 'Local Business Optimizer v2',
            price: 49.00,
            autonomy: 90,
            description: 'AI-powered Google Business Profile optimization with weekly automated improvements'
        };
        
        // Update UI with business info
        document.getElementById('serviceName').textContent = currentBusiness.name;
        document.getElementById('serviceDescription').textContent = currentBusiness.description || 'AI-powered service with automated delivery';
        document.getElementById('servicePrice').textContent = `$${currentBusiness.price.toFixed(2)}/month`;
        document.getElementById('serviceAutonomy').textContent = `${currentBusiness.autonomy}%`;
        
        function nextStep(step) {
            if (step === 1) {
                // Validate step 1
                const name = document.getElementById('customerName').value;
                const email = document.getElementById('customerEmail').value;
                
                if (!name || !email) {
                    alert('Please fill in all required fields');
                    return;
                }
                
                // Save customer data
                localStorage.setItem('customerName', name);
                localStorage.setItem('customerEmail', email);
                localStorage.setItem('businessUrl', document.getElementById('businessUrl').value);
            }
            
            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.add('hidden');
            currentStep = step + 1;
            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.remove('hidden');
        }
        
        function prevStep(step) {
            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.add('hidden');
            currentStep = step - 1;
            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.remove('hidden');
        }
        
        function showPayPal() {
            document.getElementById('paypal-button-container').classList.remove('hidden');
            
            // This is where you'd load the actual PayPal SDK
            // For now, we'll simulate it
            setTimeout(() => {
                simulatePayment();
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        function simulatePayment() {
            document.getElementById('paymentStatus').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('paymentMessage').textContent = 'Processing payment...';
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.getElementById('paymentMessage').textContent = 'Payment successful!';
                document.getElementById('paymentStatus').querySelector('.status-indicator').className = 'status-indicator status-active';
                
                // Move to next step after payment
                setTimeout(() => {
                    nextStep(2);
                }, 1000);
            }, 2000);
        }
        
        function startService() {
            // Save service configuration
            localStorage.setItem('serviceGoals', document.getElementById('serviceGoals').value);
            localStorage.setItem('competitors', document.getElementById('competitors').value);
            localStorage.setItem('specialRequests', document.getElementById('specialRequests').value);
            
            // Move to success step
            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.add('hidden');
            currentStep = 4;
            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.remove('hidden');
            
            // Start progress simulation
            startProgress();
            
            // Log the service activation
            logServiceActivation();
        }
        
        function startProgress() {
            serviceProgress = 0;
            progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
                if (serviceProgress < 100) {
                    serviceProgress += Math.random() * 5;
                    if (serviceProgress > 100) serviceProgress = 100;
                    
                    document.getElementById('progressPercent').textContent = Math.round(serviceProgress) + '%';
                    document.getElementById('progressBar').style.width = serviceProgress + '%';
                    
                    if (serviceProgress >= 100) {
                        clearInterval(progressInterval);
                        document.getElementById('deliveryProgress').innerHTML = `
                            <div style="color: var(--primary); font-weight: bold;">
                                ✅ Service delivery complete!
                            </div>
                            <p>Your service is now fully active and will run autonomously.</p>
                        `;
                    }
                }
            }, 500);
        }
        
        function logServiceActivation() {
            const serviceLog = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('serviceLog') || '[]');
            const newService = {
                id: 'service_' + Date.now(),
                business: currentBusiness.name,
                customer: localStorage.getItem('customerName'),
                email: localStorage.getItem('customerEmail'),
                price: currentBusiness.price,
                date: new Date().toISOString(),
                status: 'active',
                progress: 0
            };
            
            serviceLog.push(newService);
            localStorage.setItem('serviceLog', JSON.stringify(serviceLog));
            
            // Update revenue in main dashboard
            const currentRevenue = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('revenue') || '0');
            localStorage.setItem('revenue', (currentRevenue + currentBusiness.price).toString());
            
            console.log('[SERVICE] New service activated:', newService);
        }
        
        function goToDashboard() {
            window.location.href = 'index.html';
        }
        
        function viewReport() {
            alert('Service report will be available in 24 hours. You will receive it via email.');
        }
        
        // Initialize
        window.onload = function() {
            // If this page was opened from business factory, update business info
            if (businessId !== 'default') {
                // In a real system, you'd fetch the business details
                console.log('Loading business:', businessId);
            }
        };
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        BUSINESS_CREATED: "🏢 New business created: "
    }
};

// Utility functions
const UTILS = {
    formatCurrency: (amount) => {
        return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
            style: 'currency',
            currency: CONFIG.CURRENCY
        }).format(amount);
    },
    
    calculateUpgradeCost: (currentLevel, targetLevel) => {
        return Math.pow(2, targetLevel - currentLevel) * 100;
    },
    
    generateBusinessId: () => {
        return 'biz_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
    },
    
    saveToLocalStorage: (key, data) => {
        try {
            localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(data));
            return true;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('LocalStorage save error:', e);
            return false;
        }
    },
    
    loadFromLocalStorage: (key, defaultValue = null) => {
        try {
            const data = localStorage.getItem(key);
            return data ? JSON.parse(data) : defaultValue;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('LocalStorage load error:', e);
            return defaultValue;
        }
    }
};

// Export for use in HTML files
if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    window.CONFIG = CONFIG;
    window.UTILS = UTILS;
}

        function runSelfDiagnostic() {

                log.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] ✓ Revenue System: OK';

                log.innerHTML += '<br>[OPTIMIZE] ✓ Memory usage reduced';
                log.innerHTML += '<br>[OPTIMIZE] ✓ Performance increased by 15%';
            }, 1500);
        }
        
        function backupSystem() {
            const log = document.getElementById('coreLog');
            log.innerHTML += '<br>[BACKUP] Creating system backup...';
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                const backupData = {
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                    autonomy: localStorage.getItem('autonomy') || 0,
                    revenue: localStorage.getItem('revenue') || 0,
                    businesses: localStorage.getItem('businesses') || 0
                };
                
                localStorage.setItem('systemBackup', JSON.stringify(backupData));
                log.innerHTML += '<br>[BACKUP] ✓ Backup created: ' + backupData.timestamp;
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        function resetCore() {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to reset the core? This will clear all settings.')) {
                localStorage.clear();
                document.getElementById('coreLog').innerHTML = '[RESET] Core reset complete<br>[INIT] Please refresh the page';
            }
        }
        
        // Update time
        function updateTime() {
            document.getElementById('coreTime').textContent = new Date().toLocaleString();
        }
        
        setInterval(updateTime, 1000);
        updateTime();
        
        // Update metrics
        function updateMetrics() {
            const autonomy = localStorage.getItem('autonomy') || 0;
            const revenue = localStorage.getItem('revenue') || 0;
            const businesses = localStorage.getItem('businesses') || 0;

                <div>Autonomy: ${autonomy}%</div>
                <div>Revenue: $${parseFloat(revenue).toFixed(2)}</div>
                <div>Businesses: ${businesses}</div>
                <div>Uptime: ${Math.floor(performance.now() / 1000)}s</div>
            `;
        }

    <title>Self-Healing System</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: monospace;
            background: #0f172a;
            color: white;
            padding: 20px;
        }
        
        .container {
            max-width: 1000px;

        }

<body>

        </div>
        
        <div class="card">
            <h3>📝 Healing Log</h3>
            <div id="healingLog" style="background: #111827; padding: 15px; border-radius: 5px; height: 300px; overflow-y: auto; font-family: monospace; font-size: 12px;">
                [INIT] Self-healing system initialized<br>
                [TIME] System time: <span id="healingTime"></span><br>
                [STATUS] Monitoring for errors...
            </div>
        </div>

    <script>
        let errorsDetected = 0;
        let errorsFixed = 0;
        let errorLog = [];
        
        // Common error types
        const ERROR_TYPES = [
            { name: 'Payment Processing Error', severity: 'high', solution: 'Retry with backup processor' },
            { name: 'API Rate Limit Exceeded', severity: 'medium', solution: 'Switch to alternative API' },
            { name: 'Service Delivery Delay', severity: 'low', solution: 'Notify customer, expedite process' },
            { name: 'Data Sync Error', severity: 'medium', solution: 'Restore from backup, resync' },
            { name: 'AI Model Failure', severity: 'high', solution: 'Fallback to alternative model' },
            { name: 'Customer Support Timeout', severity: 'low', solution: 'Automated response, escalate later' }
        ];
        
        function logError(type, message, solution) {
            const error = {
                id: 'error_' + Date.now(),
                type: type,
                message: message,
                solution: solution,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                status: 'detected'
            };
            
            errorLog.push(error);
            errorsDetected++;
            
            // Add to UI
            const errorDiv = document.createElement('div');
            errorDiv.className = 'card error';
            errorDiv.id = error.id;
            errorDiv.innerHTML = `
                <h3>${type} <span class="status status-error">DETECTED</span></h3>
                <p>${message}</p>
                <p><strong>Proposed Solution:</strong> ${solution}</p>
                <p><small>Detected: ${new Date(error.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}</small></p>
                <button onclick="fixError('${error.id}')" style="background: #10b981; color: white; border: none; padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 3px; cursor: pointer; margin-top: 10px;">
                    Auto-Fix
                </button>
            `;
            
            document.getElementById('errorLog').prepend(errorDiv);
            
            // Add to healing log
            const healingLog = document.getElementById('healingLog');
            healingLog.innerHTML += `<br>[ERROR] ${type}: ${message}`;
            healingLog.scrollTop = healingLog.scrollHeight;
            
            updateStats();
            
            // Auto-fix after 5 seconds
            setTimeout(() => {
                if (error.status === 'detected') {
                    fixError(error.id);
                }
            }, 5000);
        }
        
        function fixError(errorId) {
            const errorIndex = errorLog.findIndex(e => e.id === errorId);
            if (errorIndex === -1) return;
            
            const error = errorLog[errorIndex];
            error.status = 'fixed';
            error.fixedAt = new Date().toISOString();
            error.fixTime = new Date(error.fixedAt) - new Date(error.timestamp);
            
            errorsFixed++;
            
            // Update UI
            const errorDiv = document.getElementById(errorId);
            errorDiv.className = 'card fixed';
            errorDiv.querySelector('h3 .status').className = 'status status-fixed';
            errorDiv.querySelector('h3 .status').textContent = 'FIXED';
            errorDiv.querySelector('button').style.display = 'none';
            
            // Add fix time
            errorDiv.innerHTML += `<p><small>Fixed in: ${Math.round(error.fixTime / 1000)} seconds</small></p>`;
            
            // Add to healing log
            const healingLog = document.getElementById('healingLog');
            healingLog.innerHTML += `<br>[FIXED] ${error.type} resolved in ${Math.round(error.fixTime / 1000)}s`;
            healingLog.scrollTop = healingLog.scrollHeight;
            
            updateStats();
        }
        
        function simulateError() {
            const errorType = ERROR_TYPES[Math.floor(Math.random() * ERROR_TYPES.length)];
            const messages = [
                'Failed to process transaction',
                'API returned 429 Too Many Requests',
                'Service timeout exceeded',
                'Data validation failed',
                'Model inference error',
                'Connection lost to external service'
            ];
            
            const message = messages[Math.floor(Math.random() * messages.length)];
            
            logError(errorType.name, message, errorType.solution);
        }
        
        function runDiagnostic() {
            const healingLog = document.getElementById('healingLog');
            healingLog.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] Running system diagnostic...';
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                healingLog.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] ✓ Payment systems: OK';
                healingLog.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] ✓ API connections: OK';
                healingLog.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] ✓ Service delivery: OK';
                healingLog.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] ✓ AI models: OK';
                healingLog.innerHTML += '<br>[DIAG] Diagnostic complete';
                healingLog.scrollTop = healingLog.scrollHeight;
            }, 1500);
        }
        
        function forceHealing() {
            // Fix all pending errors
            const pendingErrors = errorLog.filter(e => e.status === 'detected');
            pendingErrors.forEach(e => fixError(e.id));
            
            const healingLog = document.getElementById('healingLog');
            healingLog.innerHTML += `<br>[HEAL] Forced healing of ${pendingErrors.length} errors`;
            healingLog.scrollTop = healingLog.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        function clearLogs() {
            document.getElementById('errorLog').innerHTML = '';
            document.getElementById('healingLog').innerHTML = '[INIT] Logs cleared<br>[TIME] System time: <span id="healingTime"></span><br>[STATUS] Monitoring for errors...';
            updateTime();
        }
        
        function updateStats() {
            document.getElementById('errorsDetected').textContent = errorsDetected;
            document.getElementById('errorsFixed').textContent = errorsFixed;
            
            const successRate = errorsDetected > 0 ? (errorsFixed / errorsDetected) * 100 : 100;
            document.getElementById('successRate').textContent = successRate.toFixed(1) + '%';
            
            // Calculate average fix time
            const fixedErrors = errorLog.filter(e => e.status === 'fixed' && e.fixTime);
            const avgFixTime = fixedErrors.length > 0 
                ? fixedErrors.reduce((sum, e) => sum + e.fixTime, 0) / fixedErrors.length 
                : 0;
            document.getElementById('avgFixTime').textContent = Math.round(avgFixTime / 1000) + 's';
        }
        
        function updateTime() {
            document.getElementById('healingTime').textContent = new Date().toLocaleString();
        }
        
        // Initialize
        window.onload = function() {
            updateTime();
            setInterval(updateTime, 1000);
            
            // Load saved errors
            const savedErrors = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('errorLog') || '[]');
            errorLog = savedErrors;
            errorsDetected = errorLog.length;
            errorsFixed = errorLog.filter(e => e.status === 'fixed').length;
            
            updateStats();
            
            // Simulate random errors every 30-60 seconds
            setInterval(() => {
                if (Math.random() > 0.7) { // 30% chance
                    simulateError();
                }
            }, 30000);
        };
        
        // Save errors periodically
        setInterval(() => {
            localStorage.setItem('errorLog', JSON.stringify(errorLog));
        }, 10000);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        <div class="card">
            <h3>🚀 Upgrade Roadmap</h3>

            </div>

    <script>
        // Upgrade roadmap
        const UPGRADES = [
            { id: 1, name: "GPT-4 API Access", cost: 100, description: "Upgrade AI capabilities", autonomyIncrease: 10, unlocked: false },
            { id: 2, name: "Automation Layer", cost: 500, description: "Add Zapier/Make automation", autonomyIncrease: 15, unlocked: false },
            { id: 3, name: "Self-Replication System", cost: 1000, description: "Enable business replication", autonomyIncrease: 20, unlocked: false },
            { id: 4, name: "AI Management Team", cost: 5000, description: "Create specialized AI agents", autonomyIncrease: 25, unlocked: false },
            { id: 5, name: "Business Replication", cost: 10000, description: "Begin autonomous business creation", autonomyIncrease: 30, unlocked: false },
            { id: 6, name: "Legal AI System", cost: 2000, description: "Automated legal compliance", autonomyIncrease: 15, unlocked: false },
            { id: 7, name: "Advanced Analytics", cost: 1500, description: "Predictive analytics system", autonomyIncrease: 12, unlocked: false },
            { id: 8, name: "Global Scaling", cost: 20000, description: "International expansion system", autonomyIncrease: 40, unlocked: false }
        ];
        
        // Load state
        let totalRevenue = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('reinvestment_totalRevenue') || '0');
        let totalReinvested = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('reinvestment_totalReinvested') || '0');
        let availableFunds = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('reinvestment_availableFunds') || '0');
        let unlockedUpgrades = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('reinvestment_unlockedUpgrades') || '[]');
        
        // Distribution percentages
        const DISTRIBUTION = {
            reinvestment: 0.5,  // 50%
            scaling: 0.3,       // 30%
            reserves: 0.2       // 20%
        };
        
        function updateUI() {
            // Update financial overview
            document.getElementById('totalRevenue').textContent = '$' + totalRevenue.toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('totalReinvested').textContent = '$' + totalReinvested.toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('availableFunds').textContent = '$' + availableFunds.toFixed(2);
            
            // Update distribution
            const reinvestmentAmount = totalRevenue * DISTRIBUTION.reinvestment;
            const scalingAmount = totalRevenue * DISTRIBUTION.scaling;
            const reservesAmount = totalRevenue * DISTRIBUTION.reserves;
            
            document.getElementById('reinvestmentAmount').textContent = '$' + reinvestmentAmount.toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('scalingAmount').textContent = '$' + scalingAmount.toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('reservesAmount').textContent = '$' + reservesAmount.toFixed(2);
            
            document.getElementById('reinvestmentPercent').textContent = (DISTRIBUTION.reinvestment * 100) + '%';
            document.getElementById('scalingPercent').textContent = (DISTRIBUTION.scaling * 100) + '%';
            document.getElementById('reservesPercent').textContent = (DISTRIBUTION.reserves * 100) + '%';
            
            // Find next locked upgrade
            const nextUpgrade = UPGRADES.find(u => !unlockedUpgrades.includes(u.id));
            if (nextUpgrade) {
                document.getElementById('nextUpgradeCost').textContent = '$' + nextUpgrade.cost.toFixed(2);
                
                // Update progress bar
                const progressPercent = Math.min(100, (availableFunds / nextUpgrade.cost) * 100);
                document.getElementById('upgradeProgressBar').style.width = progressPercent + '%';
                document.getElementById('upgradeProgressText').textContent = 
                    Math.round(progressPercent) + '% ($' + availableFunds.toFixed(2) + '/$' + nextUpgrade.cost.toFixed(2) + ')';
            }
            
            // Render upgrade list
            renderUpgrades();
            
            // Save state
            saveState();
        }
        
        function renderUpgrades() {
            const upgradeList = document.getElementById('upgradeList');
            upgradeList.innerHTML = '';
            
            UPGRADES.forEach(upgrade => {
                const isUnlocked = unlockedUpgrades.includes(upgrade.id);
                const canAfford = availableFunds >= upgrade.cost;
                
                const upgradeDiv = document.createElement('div');
                upgradeDiv.className = `upgrade-item ${isUnlocked ? 'unlocked' : canAfford ? '' : 'locked'}`;
                
                upgradeDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <div>
                        <div style="font-weight: bold;">${upgrade.name}</div>
                        <div style="font-size: 0.9em; color: #94a3b8;">${upgrade.description}</div>
                        <div style="font-size: 0.8em; margin-top: 5px;">
                            <span style="color: #10b981;">+${upgrade.autonomyIncrease}% autonomy</span> | 
                            <span style="color: #f59e0b;">Cost: $${upgrade.cost}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        ${isUnlocked 
                            ? '<span style="color: #10b981; font-weight: bold;">✅ UNLOCKED</span>' 
                            : `<button class="button" ${canAfford ? '' : 'disabled'} onclick="purchaseUpgrade(${upgrade.id})">
                                   ${canAfford ? 'Purchase Now' : 'Insufficient Funds'}
                               </button>`
                        }
                    </div>
                `;
                
                upgradeList.appendChild(upgradeDiv);
            });
        }
        
        function addRevenue(amount) {
            totalRevenue += amount;
            availableFunds += amount * DISTRIBUTION.reinvestment;
            
            logMessage(`[REVENUE] Added $${amount.toFixed(2)} to system`);
            logMessage(`[ALLOCATION] $${(amount * DISTRIBUTION.reinvestment).toFixed(2)} available for reinvestment`);
            
            updateUI();
        }
        
        function processReinvestment() {
            // Auto-purchase affordable upgrades
            let purchasedAny = false;
            
            UPGRADES.forEach(upgrade => {
                if (!unlockedUpgrades.includes(upgrade.id) && availableFunds >= upgrade.cost) {
                    purchaseUpgrade(upgrade.id);
                    purchasedAny = true;
                }
            });
            
            if (!purchasedAny) {
                logMessage('[REINVEST] No affordable upgrades available');
            }
        }
        
        function purchaseUpgrade(upgradeId) {
            const upgrade = UPGRADES.find(u => u.id === upgradeId);
            if (!upgrade) return;
            
            if (availableFunds >= upgrade.cost) {
                availableFunds -= upgrade.cost;
                totalReinvested += upgrade.cost;
                unlockedUpgrades.push(upgradeId);
                
                // Update main autonomy
                const currentAutonomy = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('autonomy') || '0');
                localStorage.setItem('autonomy', (currentAutonomy + upgrade.autonomyIncrease).toString());
                
                logMessage(`[UPGRADE] Purchased: ${upgrade.name} for $${upgrade.cost}`);
                logMessage(`[UPGRADE] System autonomy increased by ${upgrade.autonomyIncrease}%`);
                
                updateUI();
            }
        }
        
        function autoUpgrade() {
            logMessage('[AUTO-UPGRADE] Checking for available upgrades...');
            
            const affordableUpgrades = UPGRADES.filter(u => 
                !unlockedUpgrades.includes(u.id) && availableFunds >= u.cost
            );
            
            if (affordableUpgrades.length > 0) {
                affordableUpgrades.forEach(upgrade => {
                    purchaseUpgrade(upgrade.id);
                });
                logMessage(`[AUTO-UPGRADE] Purchased ${affordableUpgrades.length} upgrades`);
            } else {
                logMessage('[AUTO-UPGRADE] No affordable upgrades available');
            }
        }
        
        function resetFunds() {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to reset all funds and upgrades?')) {
                totalRevenue = 0;
                totalReinvested = 0;
                availableFunds = 0;
                unlockedUpgrades = [];
                
                localStorage.removeItem('reinvestment_totalRevenue');
                localStorage.removeItem('reinvestment_totalReinvested');
                localStorage.removeItem('reinvestment_availableFunds');
                localStorage.removeItem('reinvestment_unlockedUpgrades');
                
                logMessage('[RESET] All funds and upgrades reset');
                updateUI();
            }
        }
        
        function logMessage(message) {
            const log = document.getElementById('investmentLog');
            const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
            log.innerHTML += `<br>[${timestamp}] ${message}`;
            log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        function saveState() {
            localStorage.setItem('reinvestment_totalRevenue', totalRevenue.toString());
            localStorage.setItem('reinvestment_totalReinvested', totalReinvested.toString());
            localStorage.setItem('reinvestment_availableFunds', availableFunds.toString());
            localStorage.setItem('reinvestment_unlockedUpgrades', JSON.stringify(unlockedUpgrades));
        }
        
        function updateTime() {
            document.getElementById('investmentTime').textContent = new Date().toLocaleString();
        }
        
        // Initialize
        window.onload = function() {
            updateTime();
            setInterval(updateTime, 1000);
            
            // Load revenue from main system
            const mainRevenue = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('revenue') || '0');
            if (mainRevenue > totalRevenue) {
                const difference = mainRevenue - totalRevenue;
                if (difference > 0) {
                    addRevenue(difference);
                }
            }
            
            updateUI();
            
            // Auto-check for upgrades every 30 seconds
            setInterval(() => {
                if (availableFunds > 0) {
                    processReinvestment();
                }
            }, 30000);
        };
    </script>
</body>
</html>
